<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(true)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'VendorInvoiceDataView', GridHeight: '500', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__VendorInvoiceDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '500', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'VendorInvoiceDataView', GridHeight: '500', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'VendorInvoiceDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__VendorInvoiceDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__VendorInvoiceDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__VendorInvoiceDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__VendorInvoiceDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'VendorInvoiceDataView', GridHeight: '500', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_VendorInvoiceDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divVendorInvoiceDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___VendorInvoiceDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'VendorInvoiceDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_VendorInvoiceDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "VendorInvoiceDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("VendorInvoiceDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView();
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("XLS");
    });

    $('#ExportToPdf__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView();
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("PDF");
    });

    $('#ClearSearchSettings__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDataView()
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearFilterData();
        $('#divOptions__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("padding-left", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("margin-right", "3px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__VendorInvoiceDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___VendorInvoiceDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("VendorInvoiceDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__VendorInvoiceDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__VendorInvoiceDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__VendorInvoiceDataView() {
        var gridName = 'VendorInvoiceDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___VendorInvoiceDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_VendorInvoiceDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "VendorInvoiceDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_VendorInvoiceDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__VendorInvoiceDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    $("#btnAttachments__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        NavigateTo("/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/Attachments" + "/" + selectedRowIds);
    });




    function ReturnFromVendorInvoice() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "VendorInvoiceDataView");
    }



    function EditVendorInvoiceFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: id, origin: 1, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowInvoicePopup")
           .SetIsModal(true)
           .SetContent(options)
           .SetWidth(900)
           .SetHeight("90%")
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
           .SetonClose(ReturnFromVendorInvoice)
           .SetTitle('Edit Invoice')
           finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }


    function EditVendorInvoicePopup(Id)
    {
        var grid = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditVendorInvoiceFinsWindow(Id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    $("#btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var data, options;

        data = { origin: 1 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CreateInvoicePopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowInvoicePopup")
            .SetIsModal(true)
            .SetContent(options)
            .SetWidth(900)
            .SetHeight("90%")
            .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            .SetonClose(ReturnFromVendorInvoice)
            .SetTitle('Add Invoice');
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    });

    $("#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditVendorInvoiceFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });


    $('#btnEditAll__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }

        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        if (aptaDataViewSelection.SelectedRecords !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__VendorInvoiceDataView').click();
        }

        $('#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDataView').click();
    });

    function EditVendorInvoice(selectedRowId) {
        NavigateTo("/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/Detail" + "/" + selectedRowId);
    }

    $("#btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if ($("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/GetVendorInvoiceSelectedCount",

                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", result.Message, DeleteInvoice);
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    }
                }
            });

        }

    });

    function RefreshOnDeleteInvoice()
    {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        var key = 'VendorInvoiceDataView';
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DeleteVendorInvoice',
                     { vendorInvoiceIds: selectedRowIds, operationResultId: massOperationId, key: key },
                key, function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteInvoice() {
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteInvoice(); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    $("#btnDiscountPremium__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/IsInvoiceStatusNew",
            data: { invoiceId: selectedRowIds },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var data, options;
                    data = { invoiceId: selectedRowIds };
                    options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DiscountPremium", data: data, type: "POST" };

                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowDiscountPremiumInvoice")
                     .SetIsModal(true)
                     .SetContent(options)
                    .SetWidth(600)
                    .SetHeight(260)
                    .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetTitle('Apply Discount/Premium')
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "DiscountPremiumVendorInvoice", null);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnSetInvoicedQuantities__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
        var Ids = selectedRowIds.split(",");
        var invoiceType = "";

        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
            if ($.inArray(gridData[i].Id, Ids) !== -1) {
                invoiceType = gridData[i].InvoiceType;
                if (invoiceType !== "Regular") {
                    ShowOkDialog("Selection", "This option is only available for Regular invoice types.", null);
                    return;
                }
            }
        }

        // see if the vendor invoice is not of InvoiceType == "Regular" then show error message

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/IsInvoiceItemListEmpty",
            data: { invoiceId: selectedRowIds },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {

             var data, options;

            data = { invoiceId: selectedRowIds };
            options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/SetInvoicedQuantities", data: data, type: "POST" };

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowInvoicedQuantities")
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetContent(options)
                .SetWidth(500)
                .SetHeight(150)
                .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                .SetTitle('Set Invoiced Quantities')
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "InvoicedQuantitiesVendorInvoice", null);


                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnPOBalance__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var poId;
        var poNumber;
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();

        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
            if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds) {
                poId = gridData[i].POId;
                poNumber = gridData[i].PONumber;
            }
        }

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/OpenPOBalance",
            data: { poId: poId },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowPOBalance")
                            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/POBalance?" + "poId=" + poId }).SetIsModal(true)
                            .SetTitle('PO Balance - ' + poNumber).SetonDeactivate(function () { UnRegisterActiveScreen(); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "VendorInvoicePOBalance", null);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    });

        function RefreshCopyVendorInvoice() {

                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;
    var submitForAllNoOR = false;
    var submitForAllYesOR = false;
    $("#btnSubmitForPayment__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        submitForAllNo = false;
        submitForAllYes = false;
        submitForAllNoOR = false;
        submitForAllYesOR = false;

        if ($("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Submit", "Are you sure you want to submit the selected invoice(s)?", function () { CreateFinsWindowInvoiceForSubmit(); });
        }
    });

    function CreateFinsWindowInvoiceForSubmit()
    {

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(-1, false, false, 'VendorInvoiceDataView', false, false); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    var finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO = null;

    function RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(invoiceId, overbudget, moveNext, key, associatedOrderReceipt, operationCancelled) {
        var operationResultId = GetMassActionId();
        finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowCloseInvoicePO")
                                                    .SetContent({ url:"/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/ClosePO"}).SetIsModal(true)
            .SetTitle("Close Dollar PO").SetonClose(function () { ShowResultGrid(); }).SetWidth(1000).SetHeight("65%").SetonRefresh(function () {
                                            $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/SubmitForPayment',
                         { invoiceId: invoiceId, overBudget: overbudget, moveNext: moveNext, operationResultId: operationResultId, key: key, associatedOrderReceipt : associatedOrderReceipt, operationCancelled : operationCancelled },
                    key, function (result) {
                        if(submitForAllYesOR)
                        {
                            associatedOrderReceipt = true;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            associatedOrderReceipt = false;
                        }

                        if (result.Success == 1) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key, associatedOrderReceipt, false);

                        } else if (result.Success == 3) {

                            if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                                RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key, true, false);
                            }
                            else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                                RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key, true, false);
                            }
                            else {
                                // Fix grammar error coming from database
                                result.Message = result.Message.replace("The invoice of", "The invoice");

                                if (1 == true)
                                {
                                    ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Vendor Invoice", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key, true, false); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key, true, false); submitForAllNo = e; });
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    // create an appropriate error message
                                    var intStartIndex = result.Message.indexOf("Do you wish to submit for payment anyway?");
                                    var strOverBudgetMessage = result.Message.substring(0, intStartIndex-1);
                                    strOverBudgetMessage += "&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;This Invoice cannot be submitted for payment.";
                                    ShowOkDialog("Vendor Invoice", strOverBudgetMessage, null);
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        else if (result.Success == 5) {
                            if (submitForAllYesOR === true) {
                                RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key, true, false);
                            }
                            else if (submitForAllNoOR === true) {
                                RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key, false, true);
                            }
                            else {
                                ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Vendor Invoice", "This invoice does not have a related Order Receipt for the items being invoiced. This invoice will be placed in the Pending state until an Order Receipt is created and submitted. You can submit this invoice a second time, which will create a Pending Order Receipt in the Receiving module.", function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key, true, false); submitForAllYesOR = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key, false, true); submitForAllNoOR = e; });
                            }
                        }
                        else if (result.Success == 4) {

                            //4 indicates process end,
                            submitForAllNo = false;
                            submitForAllYes = false;
                            submitForAllNoOR = false;
                            submitForAllYesOR = false;
                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                            var VendorInvoiceCloseGrid = $("#VendorInvoiceClosePODataView").data("kendoGrid");

                            VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.bind("change", function(){
                                if(VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.data().length &gt; 0){
                                    if(finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO != null)
                                        finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO.OpenWindow();
                                }
                                else{
                                    ShowResultGrid();
                                }

                            });
                            VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.read();

                        }
                        else {
                            RefreshOnSubmitForPayment(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key, true, false);

                        }
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);

                                        });
        finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO.CreateWindow(false);

    }

    function ShowResultGrid()
    {
        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');
    }

    $("#btnCancelVendorInvoice__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        if ($("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Cancel", "Are you sure that you want to cancel the selected Invoice(s)? Cancellation cannot be undone.", function(){
                                                                                                                                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshCancelVendorInvoice(); })
                                                                                                                                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                                                                                                                                });
        }
    });

    function RefreshCancelVendorInvoice() {

        var key = 'VendorInvoiceDataView';
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CancelVendorInvoice',
                { operationResultId: massOperationId, key: key, aptaDataViewSelection: $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection() },

                    var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function RefreshOnUndoSubmitForPayment()
    {

        var key = 'VendorInvoiceDataView';
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/UndoSubmitForPayment',

                    var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");

    }

    $("#btnUndoSubmitForPayment__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        if (!$("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnUndoSubmitForPayment(); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    });

    $("#btnExpressWarrantPrinting__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowId)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

                $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/IsInvoiceStatusNew",
            data: { invoiceId: selectedRowId },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var data, options;
                    data = { invoiceId: selectedRowId };
                    options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/ExpressWarrantPrintingDialog", data: data, type: "POST" };
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowExpressWarrantPrinting")
                     .SetIsModal(true)
                     .SetContent(options)
                     .SetWidth(450)
                     .SetHeight(300)
                     .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetTitle('Express Warrant Printing')
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "ExpressWarrantPrintingVendorInvoice", null);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    });

    function EditPurchaseOrder(id)
    {
        ShowPODetailPopup("/QAAutom/Purchasing/PurchaseOrder/PODetails" + "?id=" + id ,'Purchase Order Details');

    }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>

    var loadTabPODetail = true;
    var loadTabInvoiceItems = true;
    var loadTabAttachmentView = true;

    function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabStripText = $("#tabstripVI").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText()

        if (activeTabStripText == 'Invoice Items') {

            if (loadTabInvoiceItems) {
                if (loadTabInvoiceItems &amp;&amp; '0' &gt; 0) {
                    LoadGridOnDemand__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView();
                    loadTabInvoiceItems = false;
                }
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("VendorInvoiceDetailPopup", "VendorInvoiceDataView", "VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");
        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == 'PO Detail') {

            if (loadTabPODetail) {
                    LoadGridOnDemand__PODetailForInvoicesDataView();
                    loadTabPODetail = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("VendorInvoiceDetailPopup", "VendorInvoiceDataView", "PODetailForInvoicesDataView");
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Attached Files') {
            if (loadTabAttachmentView) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataView();
                var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                grid.dataSource.read();
                loadTabAttachmentView = false;
            }
            ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView")
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "VendorInvoiceDataView", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__VendorInvoice");
        }

    }

    function ShowhHidePurchaseOrder() {
        switch ($("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
            case "R":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').show();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                    break;
                }
            case "D":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').hide();
                    break;
                }
            case "C":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').show();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                    break;
                }
            case "E":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').hide();
                    break;
                }
            default:
                {
                    break;
                }
        }
    }

    function OnInvoiceTypeChange() {
        switch ($("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
            case "R":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').show();

                    $('label[for="POId"]').addClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");

                    $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').hide();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').show();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                    $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                    break;
                }
            case "D":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').hide();

                    $('label[for="POId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').addClass("RequiredLabel");

                    $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').hide();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').show();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                    break;
                }
            case "C":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').show();

                    $('label[for="POId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').addClass("RequiredLabel");

                    $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').hide();
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                    $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').show();
                    break;
                }
            case "E":
                {
                    $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="POId"]').hide();

                    $('label[for="POId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').addClass("RequiredLabel");

                    $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                    $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').show();

                    $("#OrderingVendorId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                    $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').hide();
                    break;
                }
            default:
                {
                    break;
                }
        }
    }


    var _vendorId = -1;
    var fromVendorChange = false;

    function OnPOChange() {

        var poId = $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;

        if (poId != "") {
            var data = { poId: poId };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/GetPOOrderingVendor',
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'JSON',
                data: data,

                success: function (result) {
                    if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                        var vendorCount = $("#OrderingVendorId").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.data().length;
                        if (vendorCount == 0) {
                            $("#OrderingVendorId").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.read();
                        }

                        _vendorId = result.VendorId;
                        if ($("#OrderingVendorId").data("kendoComboBox").value() == result.VendorId) return;
                        $("#OrderingVendorId").data("kendoComboBox").text(result.VendorName);
                        $("#OrderingVendorId").val(result.VendorId);
                        $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").LastText = result.VendorName;
                        fromVendorChange = true;
                        OnOrderingVendorChange();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function OnOrderingVendorChange() {

        if ($("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").Value == "E") {
            return;
        }

        var vendorId = $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
        if (vendorId === "") {
            vendorId = null;
            $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue("");
        }
        else {
            if ("0" == 0) {
                $("#PaymentVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(vendorId);
            }
        }

        if ($("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").Value == "D") {
            return;
        }

        let cmbPONumber = $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox");
        if (cmbPONumber != null) {
            cmbPONumber.DataParameters.VendorId = vendorId;
            cmbPONumber.DataParameters.CycleId = "5";
            $("#POId").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.read();
        }

        if (cmbPONumber.Value != null &amp;&amp; !cmbPONumber.DoesValueExistInSource(cmbPONumber.Value)) {
            cmbPONumber.SetValue("");
        }
    }
</script>

    <script>

        function GetInvoiceTotalAmount() {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/GetInvoiceTotalAmount",
                data: { invoiceId: '0' },
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result !== null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                        var tot = parseFloat(result.TotalAmount);
                        tot = tot.toFixed(2);
                        $("#lblSubtotalAmount").text("$" + tot);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function ValidateVendorInvoicePopup() {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var validationMessage = '';

            var vendorId = $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;

            if (isNaN(vendorId)) { vendorId = _vendorId != -1 ? _vendorId : $("#OrderingVendorId").val() }
            $("#OrderingVendorId").val(vendorId);

            var paymentVendorId = $("#PaymentVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;

            if (isNaN(paymentVendorId)) { paymentVendorId = $("#OrderingVendorId").val() }
            $("#PaymentVendorId").val(paymentVendorId);

            var employeeId = $("#EmployeeId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;


            var pOId = $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;


            var invoiceType = $("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").Value;

            var vendorInvoiceNumber = $("#VendorInvoiceNumber").val();

            if (typeof invoiceType == 'undefined' || invoiceType == '') {
                validationMessage += "Invoice Type: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
            }

            if (vendorInvoiceNumber.length &gt; 0) {
                if ($.trim(vendorInvoiceNumber) == '') {
                    validationMessage += "Invoice Number: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
                }
            }
            else {
                validationMessage += "Invoice Number: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
            }

            switch (invoiceType) {
                case "R":
                    {
                        if ('0' == 0 &amp;&amp; (typeof pOId == 'undefined' || pOId == '')) {
                            validationMessage += "PO Number: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
                        }

                        break;
                    }
                case "D":
                    {
                        if (typeof vendorId == 'undefined' || vendorId == '' || vendorId == '-1') {
                            validationMessage += "Ordering Vendor: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                case "C":
                    {
                        if (typeof pOId == 'undefined' || pOId == '') {
                            if (typeof vendorId == 'undefined' || vendorId == '' || vendorId == '-1') {
                                validationMessage += "Ordering Vendor: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
                            }
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                case "E":
                    {
                        if (typeof employeeId == 'undefined' || employeeId == '') {
                            validationMessage += "Employee: Required." + '&lt;br /&gt;';
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                default:
                    {
                        break;
                    }
            }

            if (validationMessage != '') {
                ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error");
                return false;
            }

            return true;
        }

        function VendorInvoiceSave(saveNext, saveAdd, e) {

            if (ValidateVendorInvoicePopup() == false) {
                return;
            }

            var form = $("#FormVendorInvoice");
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: form.attr('action'),
                data: form.serialize(),
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                },
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == true) {

                        if (saveNext) {
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: '', origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                            UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                        }
                        else if (saveAdd) {
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");

                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CreateInvoicePopup", data: { origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE' } });
                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                        }

                        else if ('0' &gt; 0) {
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                                grid.dataSource.read();
                            }
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                        }
                        else {
                            var Id = result.Id;
                            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: Id, origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE' }, type: "POST" });

                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                                grid.dataSource.read();
                            }
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    }
                }
            });

        }

         function VendorInvoiceSaveBeforeAnyOperation(Operation, e) {

            if (ValidateVendorInvoicePopup() == false) {
                return;
            }

            var form = $("#FormVendorInvoice");
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: form.attr('action'),
                data: form.serialize(),
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                },
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == true) {
                        switch (Operation) {
                            case "CopyVendorInvoice":
                                {
                                    CopyVendorInvoicePopup(e);
                                    break;
                                }
                            case "SubmitForPaymentVendorInvoice":
                                {
                                    SubmitForPaymentVendorInvoicePopup(e);
                                    break;
                                }
                            default:
                                {
                                    break;
                                }
                        }
                     }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    }
                }
            });

        }

        function ProcessCancelVendorInvoicePopup(transactionDateUser, e) {
            var data = { invoiceId: '0', transactionDateUser: transactionDateUser };
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/ProcessCancelInvoicePopup",
                data: data,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                            var navigationID = '';
                            if (typeof navigationID != "undefined" &amp;&amp; navigationID != null &amp;&amp; navigationID.length &gt; 0) {
                                navigationID = '';
                            }
                            else {
                                navigationID = '0';
                            }
                            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            $("#popupWindowInvoicePopup").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: navigationID, origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                           $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    }
                }
            });
        }


        $("#btnCancelPopup__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            if ('False' == 'True')
            {
            var data, options;

            data = { invoiceId: '0' };
            options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CancelInvoice", data: data, type: "POST" };

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowCancelVendorInvoice")
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetContent(options)
                .SetWidth(450)
                .SetHeight(150)
                .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                .SetTitle('Cancel Vendor Invoice')
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "CancelVendorInvoice", null);

            }
            else {
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Cancel", "Are you sure that you want to cancel the Invoice? Cancellation cannot be undone.", function () { ProcessCancelVendorInvoicePopup(null, e); });
            }
        });

        function SubmitForPayment(overBudget, e) {
            var invoiceId = $("#InvoiceId").val();
            var data = { invoiceId: invoiceId, overBudget: overBudget };
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/SubmitForPaymentSingle",
                data: data,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Success) {
                        var bOpened = false
                        var VendorInvoiceCloseGrid = $("#VendorInvoiceClosePODataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.bind("change", function () {
                            if (VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.data().length &gt; 0) {
                                if (!bOpened) {
                                    ClosePoResultMessage = result.Message;
                                    finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO.OpenWindow();
                                    bOpened = true;
                                }
                            }
                            else {
                                var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                                $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: invoiceId, origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
                                ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                            }
                        });
                        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid != null)
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        VendorInvoiceCloseGrid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    else {
                        if (result.Message.indexOf("Do you wish to submit for payment anyway?", "error") &gt;= 0) {
                            if (0 == true) {
                                ShowYesNoDialog("Vendor Invoice", result.Message, function () { SubmitForPayment(true,e); });
                            }
                            else {
                                result.Message = result.Message.replace("The invoice of", "The invoice");
                                var intStartIndex = result.Message.indexOf("Do you wish to submit for payment anyway?");
                                var strOverBudgetMessage = result.Message.substring(0, intStartIndex - 1);
                                strOverBudgetMessage += "&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;This Invoice cannot be submitted for payment.";
                                ShowAjaxMessage(strOverBudgetMessage, "error");
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

        }

        function CheckForAssociatedOrderReceipt(e) {
            var invoiceId = $("#InvoiceId").val();

            var data = { invoiceId: invoiceId };
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CheckForAssociatedOrderReceipt",
                data: data,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == true) {
                        SubmitForPayment(false,e);
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowOkCancelDialog("Vendor Invoice", "This invoice does not have a related Order Receipt for the items being invoiced. This invoice will be placed in the Pending state until an Order Receipt is created and submitted. You can submit this invoice a second time, which will create a Pending Order Receipt in the Receiving module.", function () { SubmitForPayment(false, e); });
                    }

                }
            });

        }

        function SubmitForPaymentVendorInvoicePopup(e) {
            { CheckForAssociatedOrderReceipt(e); }
        }

        $("#btnSubmitForPaymentPopup__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "VendorInvoiceDetailPopup_Error");

            if ("" == "N" &amp;&amp; "0" &gt; 0) {
                VendorInvoiceSaveBeforeAnyOperation("SubmitForPaymentVendorInvoice", e)
            }
            else {
                SubmitForPaymentVendorInvoicePopup(e);
            }
        });


        function CopyVendorInvoicePopup(e) {
             var data = { invoiceId: '0' };
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CopyVendorInvoicePopup",
                data: data,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                        var navigationID = result.newInvoiceId;

                        if (navigationID != null)
                        {
                            var aptaDataViewSelection;
                            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid != null)
                            {
                                aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            }
                            else{
                                aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                            }

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: navigationID, origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");

                        if(grid != null)
                            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        }
                   }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        $("#btnCopyInvoicePopup__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {

        });

        $('#btnSave__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var selectedRowId = '';
            if (typeof selectedRowId != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowId != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowId.length &gt; 0) {
                VendorInvoiceSave(true, false, e);
            }
            else {
                VendorInvoiceSave(false, false, e);
            }
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Edit Invoice');
        });


        $('#btnSaveAndAdd__VendorInvoiceDataView').click(function (e) {
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Add Invoice')
            e.preventDefault();
            VendorInvoiceSave(false, true, e);
        });

        $("#btnCancel__VendorInvoiceDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            closeVendorInvoicePopup(e);
        });

        function closeVendorInvoicePopup(e) {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("VendorInvoiceDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (grid != null)
                ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
        }


        var invoiceId = '0';
        var invoiceStatus = '';
        var invoiceType = 'D';



        var finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO = null;

        function RefreshOnClose()
        {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divVendorInvoiceDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            $("#popupWindowInvoicePopup").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DetailPopup", data: { Id: invoiceId, origin: 'VENDOR_INVOICE', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection } });
            ShowAjaxMessage(ClosePoResultMessage, "success");
        }

        $(document).ready(function () {

            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("VendorInvoiceDetailPopup", "VendorInvoiceDataView", "VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");

            _vendorId = $("#OrderingVendorId").data("kendoComboBox").value();
            var ClosePoResultMessage;
            finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowCloseInvoicePO")
                               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/ClosePO" }).SetIsModal(true).SetIFrame(true).SetonClose(function () { RefreshOnClose();})
                               .SetTitle("Close Dollar PO").SetWidth(1000).SetHeight("65%")
                               .SetonRefresh(function () { if ($("#VendorInvoiceClosePODataView").data("kendoGrid")) { $("#VendorInvoiceClosePODataView").data("kendoGrid").dataSource.read() } });
            finspopupwindowCloseInvoicePO.CreateWindow(false);

            $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').hide();

            $('#btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').hide();
            $('#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').hide();
            $('#btnEditAll__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').hide();
            $('#btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').hide();

            if (invoiceId &gt; 0) {
                ShowhHidePurchaseOrder();
                $("#POId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                $("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);

                if ((invoiceType == "D" || invoiceType == "C" || invoiceType == "E") &amp;&amp; invoiceStatus == "N") {
                    $('#btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();
                    $('#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();
                    $('#btnEditAll__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();
                    $('#btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();
                    if (document.getElementById("btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != 'undefined')
                        CommandButtonEnterKey("#btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");
                    if (document.getElementById("btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != 'undefined')
                        CommandButtonEnterKey("#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");
                    if (document.getElementById("btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != 'undefined')
                        CommandButtonEnterKey("#btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");

                }

                if (invoiceType == "R" &amp;&amp; invoiceStatus == "N") {
                    $('#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();
                    $('#btnEditAll__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').show();

                    if (document.getElementById("btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView") != 'undefined')
                        CommandButtonEnterKey("#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");
                }

            }
            else {
                OnInvoiceTypeChange();
            }

            if (invoiceId != 0 &amp;&amp; invoiceStatus != "N") {

                $('#PaymentVendorId').data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                $("#InvoiceType").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                if (invoiceType != "E") {
                    $("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                }
                if (invoiceType == "E") {
                    $('#EmployeeId').data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                }
            }
            if (invoiceType == "E") {

                $("#EmployeeId").closest(".k-widget").show();
                $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').show();

                $("#OrderingVendorId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').hide();

                $("#POId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
                $('label[for="POId"]').hide();

                $('label[for="EmployeeId"]').addClass("RequiredLabel");
                $('label[for="POId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                $('label[for="OrderingVendorId"]').removeClass("RequiredLabel");

                $('#EmployeeId').data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
            }
            $("#VendorName").text($("#OrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").LastText);
        });

        $('#btnAdd__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
            OpenInvoiceItemPopupAddMode();

        });

        function OpenInvoiceItemPopupAddMode() {
        var data, options;

        data = { invoiceId: '0' };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/CreateInvoiceItemPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowItemDetailsPopup")
             .SetIsModal(true)
             .SetContent(options)
             .SetHeight(460)
             .SetWidth(850)
             .SetonClose(ReturnFromVendorInvoiceItem)
             .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
             .SetTitle("Add Invoice Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "VendorInvoiceDetailDataView", null);
    }

        function EditVendorInvoiceDetail(invoiceItemSequence, invoiceId) {
            var Id = 0;
            Id = invoiceId + "~" + invoiceItemSequence;
            EditInvoiceItemFinsWindow(Id, null);
        }

        function EditInvoiceItemFinsWindow(Id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: Id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };

        options = { url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/ItemDetailPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowInvoiceItemPopup")
           .SetIsModal(true)
           .SetContent(options)
            .SetHeight(460)
           .SetWidth(850)
           .SetonClose(ReturnFromVendorInvoiceItem)
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
           .SetTitle("Edit Invoice Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "VendorInvoiceDetailDataView", null);
    }

        function ReturnFromVendorInvoiceItem() {
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("VendorInvoiceDetailPopup", "VendorInvoiceDataView", "VendorInvoiceDetailDataView");
            var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }


        $('#btnEditAll__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').click();
        }
        $('#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').click();
    });

        $("#btnEdit__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divVendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditInvoiceItemFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });


        function DeleteInvoiceItem() {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/MassActionResults" }).SetonDeactivate(function () { GetInvoiceTotalAmount(); }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteInvoiceItem(); });
                finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        }

        $('#btnDelete__VendorInvoiceDetailDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            if (!$("#divVendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;
           ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected item(s)?", DeleteInvoiceItem);
        });

        function RefreshOnDeleteInvoiceItem() {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var key = '';
        $("#divVendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/AccountsPayable/VendorInvoice/DeleteVendorInvoiceItem',
            { operationResultId: massOperationId, key: key, aptaDataViewSelection: $("#divVendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection() },
                key, function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#VendorInvoiceDetailDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__VendorInvoiceClosePODataView() {

                alert("Settings__VendorInvoiceClosePODataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {

            }
        });
    }

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;

                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;

    }

    function InitializeGrid___VendorInvoiceClosePODataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'False' == 'True';
